12:["$","ul","ul-0",{"className":"ml-4 list-disc mb-4","children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"URL"}]," - 很多人认为URL和route可互换，然而React Router中却不是这样。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Location"}]," - 是React Router独有的，基于window.location的一个对象，表示当前用户所在地。他通常用来表示URL，但是会附带额外的路由信息。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Location State"}]," - 一个未被编码的URL路由位置状态。类似于路由hash或者路由parmas，不同的是state是存储在浏览器缓存中。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-3",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"History Stack"}]," - 当用户使用路由跳转时，浏览器维护一个路由栈，对于栈中的每一个路由进行追溯。如果你长按浏览器中的向后按钮，你会看到浏览器的路由跳转历史。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-4",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Client Side Routing (CSR)"}]," - 扁平化HTML文档跳转时，浏览器会自动维护一个history stack，用户侧的路由可以让开发者在不访问后端服务的前提下操作路由堆栈。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-5",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"History"}]," React Router内置对象，用户可以用它获取路由订阅信息，同时也提供了一些API来然用户操作history stack。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-6",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"History Action"}]," - history stack的操作，有Pop. Push和Replace。可使用Push来新添加一个路由入口，使用Replace也可以达到类似的效果，只是会在堆栈中替换掉当前的路由，使用Pop来获取上一个历史路由，用以浏览器返回。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-7",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Segment"}]," - 介于'/'之间的URL片段。比如，’/users/123‘就有两个片段。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-8",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Path Pattern"}]," - 带参URL。比如动态片段'/users/:userId'和星号片段'/docs/*'。是一种React Router路由的匹配模式。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-9",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Dynamic Segment"}]," - 动态片段，见上边描述。'users/:userId'可以精确匹配'users/123'."]}],"\n",["$","li","li-10",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"URL Params"}]," - 动态路由片段解析出来的路由参数。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-11",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Router"}]," - 有状态路由组件。层级嵌套使用。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-12",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Route Config"}]," - 路由树。通过匹配机制来构建路由分支。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-13",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Route"}]," - 路由元素的基础组件。有path和element两个参数。path是匹配模式，当path匹配成功后，element中的元素才会被渲染。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-14",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Nested Routes"}]," - 嵌套路由。路由可以有自己的孩子，每一个路由都定义了URL片段，单个URL可以同时匹配路由树中的多个路由。这使得可以使用outlet. 相对路由等来布局嵌套dom结构。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-15",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Relative links"}]," - 相对路由。不使用'/'开头的路由。他会继承父级路由作为前缀来进行匹配。这使得深层次的URL渲染变得容易，因为你不用再考虑如何获得完整的上下文路由了。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-16",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Match"}]," - 当路由与URL匹配时用于保存信息的对象。比如，匹配的URL参数和路径名。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-17",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Matches"}]," - 匹配当前位置的路由数组。用于嵌套路由中。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-18",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Parent Route"}]," - 父路由。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-19",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Outlet"}]," - 父路由中匹配子路由的渲染插槽。"]}],"\n",["$","li","li-20",{"className":"font-bold mb-2","children":[["$","strong","strong-0",{"className":"font-black","children":"Index Route"}]," - outlet中默认渲染的组件。"]}],"\n","$La8","\n"]}]
